Petition from Bereaved Families of Victims in the Baoshan Road Tragedy 126

Demands of Two Bereaved Families

Declaration of Two Labor Unions

Since the tragedy in the fifth district of Baoshan Road on October 1st, nearly a month has passed with little news. We have obtained correspondence from the two bereaved families jointly petitioning the clothing and military uniform tailoring labor unions involved. The main points are recorded below:

Demands of Two Bereaved Families (1) Cai Bingquan, father of the deceased Cai Yongfang,

To the Tailoring Labor Union: Bingquan, 49 years old, native of Yuyao, Zhejiang, works as a shop assistant in a rice store in his hometown, earning very little. Yongfang, 22 years old, was his only son, burdened with supporting both branches of the family. Before his death, he worked at Shi Yongji Tailoring Shop in Xingye Lane, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, for nine years, earning a monthly salary of thirty yuan. The entire family relied on the income of the father and son to support my sister-in-law, wife, daughters-in-law, and two young granddaughters. On the afternoon of October 1st at 8 pm, You Bolu, the head of the fifth district, in order to stop the unarmed masses' anti-Japanese movement, ordered the shooting, severely injuring five people and killing two. Unfortunately, my son Yongfang tragically met his fate, dying unjustly. Sadly, he was newly married and has no heir. Alas, how painful! I received a telegram and rushed to Shanghai, submitting a request to claim his body. I am endlessly grateful for the assistance of your union. However, after reading the local news in the Shanghai Shenbao newspaper on the 19th of this month regarding the District Court's handling of this case, it stated that the case must await the recovery of the injured before it can be heard. However, it will take time for the injured to recover. I am not only suffering the pain of losing my sight, but I am also staying in a foreign land with no hope of justice. Now that autumn is ending and winter is coming, my purse is empty, and I lack food and clothing, while my entire family is crying day and night, we will inevitably sit and wait for death. One person's death leads to the death of the whole family. How can I bear this scene and situation? Therefore, I earnestly request your union to sympathetically approve, find a way to send staff to guide me and accompany me to petition various government agencies, labor unions, and schools, and provide financial assistance to save us from this disaster. Both the living and the dead will be grateful. I submit this urgent plea with utmost sincerity, awaiting your response. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Tailoring Workers' Union, Cai Bingquan, father of deceased member Cai Yongfang, weeps and kowtows, October 22nd. (2) Shen Yan, mother of the deceased Shen Huilin, to the Military Uniform Labor Union: Shen Yan, 37 years old, native of Shaoxing, Zhejiang, lost her husband when her son Huilin was five years old. Before his death, he worked at the Dali Military Uniform Factory on Baoshan Road, Zhabei. At home, there was a 74-year-old grandmother, a 14-year-old younger son, and a 12-year-old adopted daughter-in-law, Chen. The family relied on the deceased son for support. We hoped that he would become successful, and that after the adopted daughter-in-law grew up and married, they would have descendants to bring joy to the elderly and comfort their lives. Unexpectedly, the evil You Bolu of the fifth district, at 8 pm on October 1st, in order to stop the unarmed masses' anti-Japanese movement, ordered the shooting, causing him to die unjustly. Alas, how painful! Since her husband's death, she had endured countless hardships, raising this son to adulthood. Now, he was brutally murdered by You Bolu, wiping out all previous efforts. Since the occurrence of this case, the family's finances have been cut off. Furthermore, because of her grief over her son's death, she is distraught and barely wants to live. Now the family is suffering even more from the pressure of life, and we will inevitably sit and wait for death. On October 19th, news reports from the District Court stated that this case must await the recovery of the five injured before it can be heard. This means that there is no hope of justice. The family is crying out in hunger and suffering greatly. We earnestly implore your union to have mercy, do your best to protect us, and find a way to rescue us, or accompany me to petition various government agencies, organizations, labor unions, and schools, and seek financial assistance to extend the life of my family. This is my earnest prayer. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Military Uniform Workers' Union, Shen Yan, mother of deceased member Shen Huilin, weeps and kowtows, October 25th.

Declaration of Two Labor Unions: The Shanghai Tailoring and Military Uniform Workers' Unions, on behalf of the bereaved families of the Baoshan Road tragedy, tearfully appeal to all sectors of society: (omitted above) On October 1st, the fifth artillery unit posted anti-Japanese propaganda, and the guards came out to obstruct them. The guard's actions were ordered by their superiors, but You reversed protected the guard who caused the incident and indiscriminately swept bullets at patriotic protesters and civilians, causing blood and flesh to fly everywhere. The Baoshan Road tragedy was turned into a bloody massacre, and the city of unjustly dead souls suddenly added ghosts filled with grievances. At the time, the deceased Cai Yongfang (member of the Tailoring Union) and Shen Huilin (member of the Military Uniform Union), along with five injured people, were victims. Cai was an only son with no brothers, and Shen's second son was too young to earn a living. From now on, these two families will be empty, leaning on their doors and yearning, shedding tears of the western river every night. Speaking of this, how can we not be heartbroken? Alas, who doesn't have parents, fearing they won't live long? Who doesn't have a spouse? (Cai Yongfang was newly married, treating his wife as a guest and friend. What grace did he have to be born, what fault to be killed?) Since the tragedy occurred, the families of the deceased have been waiting for trial in Shanghai, crying and begging for their lives, but the court still has no date for summons. The families of the deceased are almost facing starvation. One person's death leads to the death of the whole family. You's cruelty is such that even cutting off his hair is not enough to count his crimes, and eating his flesh is not enough to wash away this hatred. If justice is not carried out soon, how can we wash away national shame and appease popular anger? We hope that all party, government, and military agencies, organizations, and schools will uphold justice, share righteous indignation, and urge the court to quickly execute the criminal, and also punish the patrol officers who opened fire according to the law, and provide compensation to the families to prevent them from starving. Then, under the nine springs, the ghosts filled with grievances can be comforted, and on the three islands, no shame will be left for the Japanese devils. This is our sincere declaration.

Hangzhou Detective Wounded in Robbery Dies Yesterday Morning 127

Wife and Concubine of the Thief to be Interrogated This Morning

Dying in the Line of Duty is Truly Pitiable

The notorious thief Wu Tianbao, a native of Shaoxing, has repeatedly committed robbery and kidnapping crimes in Hangzhou and other places. He fled to Shanghai, and the Hangzhou County Public Security Bureau issued an arrest warrant for him. Based on reports from informants, Wu was hiding in Lane 1, Beidi Fang, Beidi Road, French Concession, Shanghai. The Hangzhou County Public Security Bureau prepared a document and dispatched Detective Jiang Zhongyun with informants to Shanghai. At noon the day before yesterday, they reported to the French Concession police and requested assistance in the arrest. The police chief ordered special agents Ni Jinrong and Zhao Chunsheng, along with detectives Wang Jinyu and others, to cooperate with Detective Jiang in the arrest. They entered through the back door, but Wu noticed them and ambushed at the staircase with a gun. When Detective Jiang, Ni, Zhao, and the other detectives reached the middle of the stairs, Wu opened fire downwards, shooting Detective Jiang in the throat, Detective Ni in the cheek, and a detective in the temple. They fell to the side of the stairs one after another. Wu escaped through the roof. Detective Zhao went upstairs and captured Wu's wife and concubine, confiscating a loaded handgun. They were taken to the police station for investigation. The police used cars to transport the injured to Renji Hospital for treatment. This information was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that after Jiang Zhongyun and others were admitted to the hospital, doctors performed surgery to treat them. Unfortunately, Jiang's injuries were too severe, and he died yesterday morning despite the rescue efforts. The hospital notified the police station, which dispatched detectives to transport the body to the Tongren Fu Yuan branch morgue for an autopsy. It is reported that the deceased was 27 years old this year. The police station has notified the Hangzhou County Public Security Bureau to send personnel to Shanghai to handle the funeral arrangements. Wu's wife and concubine, who were arrested, were also sent to the court for interrogation today.

Verdict on Overseas Chinese Marriage Solicitation Case 128

All Introducers Found Not Guilty

Xu Chen Sentenced to Fine for Assault

Shao Yuefeng, a native of Changzhou and director of Guangshan Hospital at 78 Xizang Road, Zhang Zhimou, a native of Guangdong, Wu Cao, a woman from Zhejiang, and Xu Chen, a woman from Jiashan, were suspected of trafficking Chen Guizhen (16 years old, a dancer at Tiandong Dance Hall) to Li Yuxuan, an overseas Chinese from Holland. Chen Yonggui, a Chinese detective from the Laoza Gate Police Station, arrested Shao and others and handed them over to the First Special District Court. Shao Yuefeng was ordered to pay a bail of 200 yuan, Xu Chen 300 yuan, and Zhang Zhimou and Wu Cao were released pending summons. This information has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Xu Jiashi of the Criminal Division of the Special Court presided over the hearing in the First Criminal Court. The police lawyer Ru Bao Yi stated that the police are now prosecuting the four defendants according to Article 257 of the Criminal Law for trafficking in persons, and additionally charging Xu Chen with Article 293 of the same law for obstruction of justice, because she injured her adopted daughter Wu Xiaomao. During the adjournment, the police inquired with the Dutch consulate, and the Dutch consul Van Dunburg replied that Li Yuxuan was indeed a widower with thirteen children at home, and his purpose for coming to Shanghai was unknown. However, Li Yuxuan did not appear in court today. Interrogated, Shao Yuefeng, Zhang Zhimou, and Wu Cao all testified that they were acting as matchmakers for Li, and there was no trafficking involved. During their testimony, Shao and Zhang addressed each other as brothers, and the sound of "brother, brother" was incessant. The police lawyer Ru interrupted them, saying that this was a court and they could not address each other as brothers. Shao and others complied, but after a short while, Shao again addressed him as brother, presumably out of habit. Interrogated, Xu Chen denied injuring Xiaomao, and said that Guizhen was her adopted daughter and she had always been very fond of her. She said that she really did not want to this time. She also hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend her. Judge Xu verified the testimony and acquitted Shao Yuefeng, Zhang Zhimou, and Wu Cao on the spot. Xu Chen was fined sixty yuan for causing bodily harm, and acquitted of the charge of enticement. Xiaomao was sent to the Jiliang Institute for care. Shao Yuefeng, suspected of false accusation, was ordered to pay an additional bail of eight hundred yuan and sent to the Prosecutor's Office for investigation.

Ye Jihong Still Hopes Li Caiying Will Reconsider 129

Unwilling to Sever Relationship

Court Orders Out-of-Court Reconciliation

Ye Jihong, a 33-year-old Shanghai resident living at 234 Huashun Lane, Tongfu Road, who works at a gold exchange, became acquainted with Li Caiying, a woman from Changzhou, in February of last year. Recently, due to disagreements, Li hired a lawyer to accuse Ye of undermining public morals and demanded to end the relationship with Ye and return clothing and jewelry worth 3,000 yuan. Yesterday, Judge Shen Bingrong of the First Special District Court presided over the hearing in the Third Criminal Court. According to Li Caiying's statement, her husband Sun Ruiqi was addicted to opium and did not engage in legitimate business, so she cohabitated with the defendant. Recently, he has not provided her with expenses, and he does not allow her to return to her hometown to visit her sick aunt. He said that if she wanted to return home, he would kill her. Therefore, she does not want to live with him. All the clothing and jewelry worth 3,000 yuan have been pawned. She requests the court to order their return and permanently sever the relationship. Interrogated, the defendant stated that when he cohabitated with her, it was introduced by someone. He has spent more than 8,000 yuan on her. Furthermore, his legal wife divorced him because of the plaintiff. He has treated her well in the past. Now that she is involved in litigation, she is listening to her mother's instructions. If she is determined to sever the relationship, he will file a counterclaim, accusing her of fraud. He hopes she will reconsider and continue to live with him. In short, he now regrets it and asks the court for a clear judgment. Judge Shen declared to the plaintiff that their type of case would be canceled. He then ordered both parties to reconcile outside of court and rescheduled the hearing.

Chen Xuchu Accused by Concubine 130

Order Rescheduled for Further Investigation

Chen Xuchu, 40 years old, the owner of the Zhongshan Hotel on Tianjin Road, was accused of undermining public morals by Zou Zhendan, 31 years old, his concubine from Changshu, who resides at 53 and a half Puqing Lane, Fujian Road. The case was filed in the First Special District Court. The case had previously been summoned once, but Chen did not appear, resulting in a postponement. The day before yesterday, Judge Shen Bingrong continued the hearing in the Third Criminal Court. According to the plaintiff Zou Zhendan's statement, her husband's surname was Gu, and they divorced in March of the 16th year of the Republic of China due to disagreements, and he paid her 5,000 yuan for living expenses. At that time, she met Chen at a large restaurant in Shanghai, and they fell in love and began cohabitating for about three years. In the past, Chen would come to her place every other night. However, on September 21st, Chen took advantage of her absence and brought more than 20 men and women, broke down the door, and forcibly moved the redwood furniture and six clothing chests from her room, hiring a car to transport them away. At that time, neighbors, seeing that she had not returned, tried to stop them. Chen patted his chest and assured them that they could speak to him if anything happened. He had previously been tricked out of his savings account, which had not yet been returned. Liu Qiufeng, the owner of the Rongji Cigarette Paper Shop next door, testified that he personally witnessed the defendant bringing dozens of men and women to break down the plaintiff's door, move out the clothing chests and furniture, and hire a car to park at the entrance of the alley to load them up, which was indeed the case. Interrogated, Chen Xuchu stated that he was engaged in miscellaneous businesses, and the Zhongshan Hotel was owned by shareholders. He had known the plaintiff for nearly three years. Previously, he had found a photograph in her bedroom drawer, in which she was with a man. She said that the man was the godfather of her daughter, but this person was her new paramour. Therefore, he obtained this evidence and stopped giving her monthly expenses. When he went to move the items from her room, he reported it to the Laoza Gate Police Station, which sent Chinese and Western detectives. Furthermore, all the redwood furniture was purchased by him. His lawyer presented the photograph of the plaintiff and the man for inspection. Zou Zhendan said that the redwood furniture in the room was actually bought with 400 yuan she made from working in Singapore from her friends. She denied knowing the man in the photograph. Judge Shen verified the testimony and ordered a rescheduling for further investigation.

Petty Inn Owner Sentenced for Enticing a Minor 131

Four Months Imprisonment

Wen Chuxi, the 20-year-old daughter of Wen Lanting, the owner of the Wen Maosheng Chicken and Duck Shop at 54 Caishi Street, French Concession, was abducted last month in collusion with Zhou Ade, the owner of the Xinsheng Petty Inn at 27 Mofang Street, and his wife Zhang. The Zhou couple were arrested by the French police detectives and handed over to the Second Special Court. Judge Ge Zhitang questioned them and ordered them to be held for further review. Yesterday, the hearing continued. Zhou Afa testified that Wen was in love with a man, who was the husband of the inn's owner, because they were sworn sisters. They exchanged gold rings in May and often went out to the cinema and opened rooms in inns. This time, it was actually Chunxi who insisted on forcing him to rent a small house outside to cohabitate with her. Later, the wife of the man found out and came to make trouble, which caused the litigation. Zhou Zhang testified that although she and Wenxi were sworn sisters, she did not know that she was having an affair with her husband. She only found out when her husband was often away from home. She did not dare to collude in the abduction. Wen Chunxi testified that although she and Zhou Zhang, also known as Ai Lin, were sworn sisters, she had no love for her husband. Ai Lin tricked her into going to her sister's place in Peiping to study, and abducted her to 7 Pingji Lane, Maithestrasse Road, where Zhou Afa forcibly raped her. Later, he tricked her out of her gold jewelry and spent it all, and wanted to force her to write a letter to her father, demanding 500 yuan. Therefore, she fled home and reported the case to the police. Next, Li Zhao, the landlady of 7 Pingji Lane, Maithestrasse Road, testified that Zhou Afa rented the floor from her at the beginning of July for 11 yuan per month, claiming that he had escaped the flood from Hankou to Shanghai. Later, on the 10th, Zhou Afa and Wen Chunxi came to live there. She mistakenly thought they were a married couple and did not know that they had been abducted. Tang Amao, the chauffeur of the Fulai Motor Car Company, and Zhang Bingsheng, Wen's brother-in-law, also testified in court to prove everything. At this point, the judge ordered the lawyers for both sides to debate. Judge Ge then announced the end of the debate and sentenced Zhou Afa to one year and six months of imprisonment for the crime of enticing a girl under the age of twenty away from the custody of her parents with the intent to commit adultery. Zhou Zhang was sentenced to four months of imprisonment for the crime of helping a person who intends to commit adultery to entice a girl under the age of twenty away from the custody of her parents. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Zhou Zhang was given a two-year suspended sentence. During the appeal period, she was ordered to pay a bail to be available for summons. Without bail, she will be temporarily detained by the police. Wen Chunxi was taken back by her father.

Motorized Bicycle Emitting Thick Smoke 132

Fine of Ten Yuan

Xu Changfa, the owner of the Wujin Store at 303 Fuxu Road, drove a No. 98 motorized bicycle on Aiduya Road in the French Concession in front of the Nanjing Grand Theater the day before yesterday. The vehicle emitted a large amount of thick smoke, which was discovered by No. 47 Western police officer Laobuxuelaofu. The officer determined that the defendant had violated Article 12 of the Traffic Regulations, which prohibits causing public nuisance. He recorded the license plate number and reported to the police chief. Yesterday, Xu was summoned to the Second Special Court for a summary trial. The police lawyer stated the facts of the case, and No. 47 Western police officer testified about the defendant's smoke emission situation at the time. Interrogated, Xu Changfa admitted to emitting smoke and said that all motorized bicycles emit smoke, not just his vehicle. He asked for leniency. The police lawyer said that although other vehicles emit smoke, none are as thick as the defendant's. Judge Wu sentenced Xu to a fine of ten yuan as a warning.

Hou Mengsheng Attacked with an Axe on the Road 133

Wounded in More Than Ten Places

Life Hanging by a Thread

Hou Mengsheng, a native cloth broker from Shengqiao, Huxi, received more than 200 silver dollars for cloth in Shanghai yesterday. On his way back in the afternoon, he was suddenly attacked from behind by an enemy with an axe in Shenjiahang and slashed more than ten times, falling to the ground wounded. The attacker fled. Hou was severely injured and unable to speak. Later, an acquaintance saw him and informed his family, who carried him home. He was barely breathing. He was taken to a hospital in Shanghai for treatment. He is said to be in critical condition. The silver dollars in his pocket were still there. His family has reported the crime to the authorities and requested that the attacker be arrested and prosecuted.

Sand Boat Crew Member Falls and is Crippled 134

Hong Dasheng, a South Gang sand boat, recently set sail for export. In order to prepare the ship, A Qing, a crew member, was hanging gourds on top of the main mast yesterday when he accidentally fell to the deck from a height. He lost consciousness instantly. His colleagues helped him up and sent him to the hospital. According to the doctor, he suffered severe internal injuries and a broken back. Although his life can be saved, he may be crippled.

Two Girls Flee Together Due to Unbearable Stepmother's Abuse 135

Zhang Gendi and Wang Guibao

Taizhou Peddler Escapes

Nian Yongfa, the police chief of the pier sub-station of the First District General Bureau of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, discovered two young women at the Dada Pier in the Sixteenth Concession at around 5:00 PM yesterday who were about to board a Taizhou steamer. Observing their panicked expressions, he suspected that there was something amiss and went forward and ordered the two women to stop. When he questioned them about their background, the two women gave evasive answers. He immediately took them back to the sub-station and transferred them to the General Bureau. During the preliminary hearing, one of the women gave her name as Zhang Gendi, 16 years old, from Suzhou, currently residing in Lan Nidu, Pudong. Both her parents are alive, but her mother is a stepmother who is fierce and impetuous. If she slightly displeases her, she will be whipped. Her father witnessed it but was naturally fearful and dared not protest, so her life was like being in a living hell. She had long planned to escape this bad family, but had no opportunity. Wang Guibao (referring to the other woman) is her neighbor. Her mother has passed away, and she is now living in the hands of her stepmother. Her suffering is similar to hers. A peddler from Taizhou, Mr. Jia, often met with them, and they felt that he was kind and gentle. Therefore, they agreed to flee together the day before yesterday. At that time, she, Guibao, and Mr. Jia secretly went to Puxi. That night, they opened a room in a hotel near the Great World in the North City to stay overnight. Mr. Jia said that since they lacked a suitable place to live at the moment, they might as well go with him to his ancestral home in Taizhou to avoid being abused by their stepmothers all day long. She and Guibao heard this and thought that since there was no place to live in Shanghai, why not follow his words and start together. Therefore, they prepared to take a steamer at the Dada Pier shortly before being discovered by the police and queried. Mr. Jia, fearing that the matter would be revealed, took the opportunity to escape. They were then brought in by the police, but their families are really too bad. If they return, they fear that their stepmothers will treat them as enemies, and they will not be able to live. They beg for understanding. Wang Guibao, when questioned, said that she was 14 years old, from Pudong, and the rest of her statement was the same as Zhang Gendi's. They are being detained for investigation and verification.

Carelessness at Xuhui Public School 136

At 11:30 PM the day before yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out in the kitchen of Xuhui Public School in the Xujiahui Catholic Church in Huxi due to an electrical short circuit. The fire quickly spread through the roof, and the firelight was blazing and uncontrollable. The cook woke up from his dream and quickly reported the fire by telephone. The fire brigades from each district arrived at the scene to fight the fire. It took three minutes to extinguish the fire. Two kitchens were burned down, with losses of several hundred yuan.

Male Corpse on the Banks of Yujiawan 137

Yesterday, a male corpse was found lying on the banks of Yujiawan. He was about 30 years old and wore a white cloth short shirt and trousers, which were old and worn. His skin was waxy yellow all over, indicating that he had been eating red pills (commonly known as opium cessation pills on rifles, which are highly toxic) for a long time, poisoning his bone marrow to death. Since he had no family, the Second District Police Department ordered Dong Jianqing, the Tu Di Bao of the fifth district, to report to the District Court for an autopsy. The corpse was then collected by the Tang for burial.

Elderly Man Found Dead on Zhonghua New Road 138

Over Seventy Years Old

Autopsy Confirms Death from Illness

An elderly man was found dead on Zhonghua New Road in Zhabei yesterday. He was over seventy years old, with white hair and beard, and his clothes were ragged, looking like a refugee. The Fifth District Police Department, as usual, ordered Huang Hongsheng, the Tu Di Bao of Jin Second District, to report to the District Court. The autopsy confirmed that he had died of illness and ordered that he be collected by a charitable organization for burial.

Two Notices from the Maritime Affairs Section of the Customs 139

Notice No. 1014 from the Marine Department of the Customs, states: This Marine Department has checked and found that the lights on the floating buoys at the Yangtze River mouth within the jurisdiction of the Jianghai Customs Service have been changed and another buoy has been added. The details are listed below: The positions of the Yangtze River mouth buoys will be changed on or about November 4th of this year. This will take effect at that time and no further notice will be given. (1) The light originally installed on the Bakou Buoy will now be changed to red. The direction and other circumstances remain the same. (2) A new buoy, decorated in red and marked with the English letter "C", called Jiuduan Shazui Buoy, will be added. It is equipped with a flashing white light, flashing once every eight seconds, i.e. flashing for four seconds and then off for four seconds, to indicate the right side of the entrance channel. From the buoy, Nanhui is located south 70 degrees and 45 minutes west (according to the compass direction), a distance of 8 miles and 94 hundredths of an English mile. Refer to Chinese Navy Chart No. 1011 for clarity. All vessels are hereby notified to comply with this notice and to pay attention to details so as to avoid errors. Do not forget this important notice. October 12th, Republic of China Year 20. Commissioner of Customs, Maritime Department, Xi Liman.

Furthermore, Notice No. 1015 states: This Marine Department has checked and found that the floating buoy marking the sunken Dachang ship within the jurisdiction of the Jianghai Customs Service has been removed. The details are listed below. The Dachang steamship sank near Wusongkou and was previously announced in Notices No. 1002 and No. 1005. Now that the sunken ship has been moved, the buoy marking the sunken ship will be removed on or about November 4th of this year. This will take effect at that time and no further notice will be given. Refer to Chinese Navy Chart No. 1011 for clarity. All vessels are hereby notified to comply with this notice and to pay attention to details so as to avoid errors. Do not forget this important notice. October 12th, Republic of China Year 20. Commissioner of Customs, Maritime Department, Xi Liman.

Cow and Chicken Essence Made with Cold Extraction Method 140

Exclusive Management by Huada Pharmacy in This Port

The Shirilike brand beef essence and chicken essence from the German Marda Pharmaceutical Factory, exclusively managed by Huada Pharmacy in this port, has been increasingly popular in recent years and has spread throughout the country. After autumn, branch managers in various ports have added goods one after another, and more than ten new branch management offices have been added, resulting in a situation where supply cannot meet demand. The reason is that Shirilike brand beef essence and chicken essence are made using the cold-pressing method invented by the technicians of the Marda Pharmaceutical Factory. Extremely large easy-pressing machines are used, with the pressure inside the machine reaching more than 27,000 pounds of meat slices. After processing by this machine, the residue becomes fine powder and is separated from the original juice. The nutrients such as protein contained in the meat are not lost at all, so the efficacy is great and has a reputation that is unique in the world, and the sales volume is increasing year by year. In these two weeks, the store sent dozens of telegrams to the German factory to urge delivery. The goods shipped from the German factory also had four batches. However, the quantity of each batch was as before, so it was still insufficient to supply. Only yesterday did a large batch five times the quantity arrive in Shanghai.

Fúmín Rice Mill Restores Former Glory 143

Two Shanghai industrialists, Mr. Zhāng Xiàoliáng and Mr. Zhōu Xuéwén, acquired dozens of acres of land seventy miles west of Shanghai in the Sìgǎngkǒu area. They built hundreds of factory buildings and machine houses, establishing the Fúmín Rice Mill. The scale is grand, and the equipment is complete, unparalleled in the Sū, Xī, Cháng, and Hù areas. The previous typhoon blew down dozens of zhang of the corridor sheds, as well as other buildings. Mr. Zhōu immediately hired workers to repair the damage, and the mill has long since restored its former glory and resumed operations as usual. It is reported that all the milling machines in the factory were ordered from famous German factories after on-site inspections. Therefore, the rice produced is particularly bright, and the amount of bran and broken rice is also less than that of other factories. Furthermore, the mill enjoys extremely convenient water and land transportation, and the authorities have assigned military police to escort merchants from various ports who come to do business. There seems to be an overwhelming demand. Yesterday, Mr. Zhōu came to Shanghai again to discuss increasing capital and vigorously promoting the business with Mr. Zhāng Xiàoliáng, which is expected to be realized soon.

This column of reader correspondence has always been limited to three issues: schooling, career, and marriage. Since the outbreak of the Japanese invasion of the Northeast, dozens of letters every day have been asking about how to resolve the Northeast problem and how to respond to Japanese atrocities. This is a passionate expression of patriotism from our compatriots, which we greatly admire. We now make an agreement with you all: Please temporarily set aside personal issues such as schooling, career, and marriage, and focus on researching methods to save the country. Please express your opinions on the following questions:

(1) What kind of position should our country take on the League of Nations to be most appropriate?

(2) What are effective and practical ways to boycott Japanese goods? (You can focus on one industry or one region.)

(3) How can the training of volunteer soldiers be expanded and sustained?

(4) How can we unite the people of the whole country to face external enemies?

Each answer should be limited to a maximum of one thousand words. Speak less empty words and focus on proposing methods. This newspaper will select and publish the best ones based on the capacity of this column and open them for public discussion. If you agree with the methods proposed by others, please also state so. Please also include your full name, gender, age, occupation or place of study, and place of origin, and attach a communication stamp and a sufficient number of postage stamps. Those who are not published in the newspaper will be notified by letter. As for the three issues of schooling, career, and marriage, they will still be handled according to the existing regulations. Sincerely,

Special Issue Commemorating the 20th Anniversary of the China Public School Industrial Society

Fundamental Methods and Policies to Be Adopted for Promoting Domestic Goods (Wú Xiàoyún) 151

Our country suffers from foreign economic aggression, exceeding 120 million yuan annually. Patriotic people are all calling for the promotion of domestic goods. For over twenty years, the results have been very limited. Foreign goods still flood the market, and domestic goods remain sluggish. The reason for this is the lack of fundamental methods and policies. The Society is requesting views from fellow citizens on this topic. We have received no less than several hundred excellent works. We select and publish the best ones for the reference of the national industrial and commercial circles. The views expressed in this article are insightful. Readers can refer to the article by Mr. Lǚ Yínshēng published in the special issue of the Shēnbào Newspaper yesterday (Editor's Note). Since the nineteenth century, domestic industries in European countries have made great strides, resulting in overcapacity of production, oversupply of products, and oversupply of raw materials; the increase in capital has also exceeded the capacity of the country, so they have had to plunder colonies to obtain raw materials; seek overseas markets to sell surplus products, and further use these conquered colonies or markets, with their abundant raw materials and cheap labor, to operate various enterprises, in order to circulate the country's surplus capital and monopolize local industries and finance, thus creating the development and aggression of imperialism. Our country is vast and populous, rich in resources, and economically backward with nascent industry and commerce, and this type of market meets the needs of imperialists. Therefore, in 1840, Britain took advantage of the victory in the Opium War to force the signing of the Treaty of Nanjing. Other powers also took the opportunity to demand the signing of various unequal treaties. Since then, our country's doors have been wide open, and the powers, with the unequal treaties as a protective talisman and the power of gunboat diplomacy, have greatly expanded their ambitions for economic aggression. In recent years, according to customs reports, the annual trade deficit is often around 100 million taels, and the profits earned by domestic and foreign merchants operating various enterprises are also no less than 100 million. Such leakage has led to the dangerous situation of economic bankruptcy, impoverishment of the people, widespread banditry, and years of disasters in our country today. People with insight all believe that the promotion of domestic goods is the only good policy to resist economic aggression and save the country from danger. However, what are the fundamental methods for promoting domestic goods? And what policies should be adopted? The author is not talented, but lists several major points as follows, hoping that the whole country will work together with one heart and one mind!

1. Social Stability

Consider the countries of Europe and America, and our eastern neighbor Japan, the basis of their national wealth and strength lies in the two major foundations of industrial development and enlightened politics. However, the prerequisite for building these two major foundations must be social stability, because social stability is the mother of construction. Once society is stable, any plan can be realized; otherwise, even construction will be in vain. Since the late Qing Dynasty, up to recent years, our country's situation has been precarious, with internal troubles and external threats, and there has been no year of peace. This phenomenon is caused by the instability of society. In these decades, the people of the country have not attempted to develop various undertakings, but what have been the achievements? What has been the result? The past is still there, and it is not difficult to review. Therefore, to stabilize the country internally and resist external forces, we must first seek to stabilize society. Once society reaches a state of stability, the power of construction will be easily and fully utilized, and the development of industry and the revitalization of domestic goods can be expected soon.

2. Abolition of Unequal Treaties

The reason why our people's livelihood is so depleted and our industry is so backward is due to the gift of unequal treaties. Imperialists use these treaties to plunder our raw materials and monopolize our markets: In particular, the clause "determining that China shall not freely increase tariffs" has put our industry and commerce in an irrecoverable situation. During the European War, the powers had no time to attend to it, and our industry and commerce temporarily showed signs of recovery. But after the end of the European War, the powers came east again with their strong economies to confront our country, but the result was not only no progress, but a disastrous defeat. The reason for this failure should be attributed to the monopoly of foreign merchants in China. If society is stable and the powers have no excuse, then it will be easy for the whole country to work together to abolish the unequal treaties. Once these treaties are abolished, foreign merchants will lose their reliance, tariffs will be controlled by us, and domestic industries will be able to develop independently, and foreign trade can also be controlled by us. With our country's vast territory and abundant resources, in accordance with Dr. Sun Yat-sen's method of "catching up with Western civilization," the development of our country's industry will be like the Yangtze River rushing thousands of miles, and the problem of people's livelihood will be solved easily, not just the promotion of domestic goods.

3. Development of Resources and Improvement of Transportation

A country's industry and commerce flourish in an environment free from internal strife and external troubles, and its progress depends on the convenience of transportation and the supply of raw materials, which go hand in hand. If one is lacking, then industry and commerce will rarely be able to develop fully. If Japan did not have coal, iron, and grain from the three eastern provinces, Japan's national defense, transportation, and even various undertakings would suffer greatly. If Britain did not have cotton from India and wool from Australia, then Britain's textile industry would be completely paralyzed. However, if the raw materials in these two places were not transported by trains and ships reaching all directions, the impact would be the same as having no raw materials. It is more difficult to seek the supply of raw materials than to seek convenient transportation, so in countries with developed industry and commerce, transportation is convenient, and the only worry is that raw materials cannot be self-sufficient. Our country is blessed by nature, and it has all the raw materials that industry needs. It is only because transportation is obstructed that they cannot be fully developed. In normal times, we can still rely on others, but if war breaks out and the source is cut off, wouldn't we be sitting and waiting for death? Writing this, I can't help but shudder! If the people of the country do not want to promote domestic goods, then so be it, otherwise, making efforts to improve transportation in order to develop resources is an urgent plan that must be taken. As for how to improve transportation and how to develop resources, Dr. Sun Yat-sen speaks in great detail in the Industrial Plan, so there is no need to repeat it.

The three major fundamental policies described above cannot be handled in a day or two. They can only be gradually realized after the country's strength is sufficient. Before the country's strength is sufficient, we cannot but prepare the following policies that are easy to implement to promote domestic goods, so as to lay the foundation for future development. 1. Training Talents

The employees of industry and commerce in the East and the West, from small workers and shop assistants to engineers and general managers, all have considerable talents to fulfill their responsibilities. This kind of talent is formed by peacetime training, so industry and commerce are making progress every day and without end. The reason why our country's industry and commerce cannot catch up quickly is not the lack of talents, but the lack of training for talents. Because the original talents are often used in positions unrelated to their studies, these talents have neglected their studies for a long time, and once they enter practical work, they want to use their strengths in the positions they hold, but because they have no considerable training in peacetime, they can only grope in the dark, which reduces work efficiency. How can we expect rapid industrial and commercial development in this way? Therefore, training talents is the first preparation for developing our industry and commerce.

2. Concentrating Capital

The reason why our country's manufacturers cannot win against foreign-funded manufacturers is mostly due to the fact that the capital is too small and the scale is too small. Since the economic ability is insufficient, there is naturally no large-scale production and great business. It is inevitable that they will be oppressed by foreign capital. Therefore, to seek the development of industry and commerce and the revitalization of domestic goods, we must concentrate a large amount of capital. Not only can we compete with foreign capital, but large-scale production can save a lot of artificial power construction and other expenses compared to small-scale production. This method is very suitable for our country's economic situation, and we hope to take action quickly.

3. Improving and Imitating

The reason why domestic goods are not as exquisite as foreign goods is not that the brains of the Chinese people are weaker than those of foreigners, but that the Chinese people are sticking to the old ways and failing to use scientific methods to improve them. In recent years, although the people of the country have spared no effort to promote domestic goods, there seems to be little progress in improving the goods. Even with silk and tea, which were the main exports of our country twenty years ago and occupied an important position in overseas markets, they have been squeezed out by Britain and Japan because they did not know how to improve them. Other things such as porcelain and silk are also declining. The plan to save them is to engage in improvement in order to achieve the effect of promotion. As for the necessities that are not unique to our country, we should actively imitate them. In terms of quantity, we must strive to be self-sufficient and no longer rely on others. If this is really the case, the leakage can be reduced, and foreign goods can be resisted.

4. Encouragement and Assistance

It is difficult to expect any undertaking to flourish without encouragement and assistance, and industry and commerce are no exception. The countries of the East and the West give comprehensive encouragement and assistance to their own industry and commerce, such as holding large-scale expositions, establishing industrial exhibition halls everywhere, increasing import taxes on foreign goods without restriction, making efforts to reduce export taxes on domestic goods, providing economic and technical assistance to private enterprises, and using all possible means to restrict and oppress foreign-funded manufacturers. All these are protection policies for their own industry and commerce. Our country cannot fully implement the protection policies described above before the unequal treaties are abolished. We are doing our best to encourage and fully assist within the possible range, so that people know the importance of developing industry and foster a psychology of being ashamed of using foreign goods. With this policy, it is not difficult to promote domestic goods. 5. Industrial and Commercial Integrity

"Merchants value profit and despise integrity," is the saying that used to despise merchants. It is more true today, as among the merchants, there are those who only know how to seek profit and disregard integrity, such as those who collude with foreign merchants to pass off imported goods as local products, those who use shareholders' capital to engage in speculative undertakings, those who disregard shareholders' interests and only seek personal pleasure, and those who adulterate inferior quality products as soon as their products gain social credibility in order to seek profits. As a result, I don't know how many manufacturers have closed down. It seems that not only is industrial and commercial integrity swept away, but the future of domestic goods is also greatly affected. However, there are also many examples of those whose business is booming because of taking care of integrity, such as the China Chemical Industry Society and the Three Friends Industrial Society, which have a history of twenty years, and all of them are "honest and un欺". If our country's manufacturers want their business to develop and last for a long time, they must pay attention to industrial and commercial integrity.

6. Labor-Capital Cooperation

The content of our country's labor problem is extremely complicated, and if handled carelessly, it will cause great disputes. In recent years, although the labor and capital sides seem to be at peace on the surface, the prejudices are deep. If it is not completely resolved, the loss to our country's industrial circles will be great. At this time when the country is in dire straits and the promotion of domestic goods is actively underway, how should the labor and capital sides understand each other and work together to develop industry and strengthen the country? Is this not only beneficial to both labor and capital?

7. Field Investigation

Closing the door to build a car may not fully meet the needs of the world: It may not be fully suitable for the use of various places in terms of manufacturing goods. Therefore, field investigation is still in need. The reason why foreign goods can cater to the tastes of the Chinese people and flood our markets is the result of foreigners coming to China to investigate. The reason why our country's native products are gradually declining overseas and almost completely replaced by foreign goods at home is that they are ignorant of the importance of investigation. From now on, if we want to develop native products abroad and resist foreign goods at home, we must send personnel to conduct field investigations. We must conduct thorough research and statistics on the social situation, the psychology of the people, and the quality and quantity of the products sold before we can gallop the business arena and victory can be manipulated, as the saying goes: Know yourself and your enemy, and you will win every battle.

A General Overview and Suggestions for the Development of China's Seasoning Industry (By Ms. Kang Pei-ying) 152

In China, the first seasoning product was the Ajinomoto from Japan. Almost every Chinese person knows about it. It rampaged through the Chinese market for twenty years, and the outflow of our money was countless. Later, domestic factories were established one after another to manufacture this product in order to resist it. Those that have achieved success include the Guanyin Powder from China Chemical Industry Society, the Hehe Powder from Gentai Factory, the Wuweisu from Defeng Factory, the Weijing from Tianchu Factory, and the Weimu from Tianyi Factory, all of which have achieved great success. But it is a pity to say that although these factories have worked hard for many years, shouting themselves hoarse to promote and publicize in order to resist foreign goods, they have only achieved the current slight success. However, their products still cannot be sold all over the country, especially in the northeastern provinces. On the one hand, the factories' capabilities are weak, and they cannot arouse the attention of the Chinese people; on the other hand, the Chinese people cannot shirk the blame for not promoting them! However, it is not too late to mend the fold after the sheep is lost. Now is the era of great competition. I sincerely hope that the factories and the Chinese people will quickly pay attention, do their best to promote them, and purchase domestic goods in groups. The winning ticket is still in our hands after all.

Speaking of seasoning powder, it is a fine powder, white in color and delicious in taste. It dissolves in water and can increase the umami flavor of all kinds of vegetables several times. In today's increasingly high-cost of living, everything is expensive, and fish, meat, and vegetables are no exception. Therefore, to solve the problem of diet and save money, seasoning powder came into being. Using a little seasoning powder in dishes can turn them into exquisite and delicious dishes, which can both increase appetite and solve economic problems. It is truly a win-win situation. Therefore, now almost every restaurant, big or small, and every household, upper, middle, or lower class, uses this product. It has undoubtedly become an indispensable item for daily use.

Since seasoning powder occupies such an important position in the national production, then we cannot but pay attention to its future when this seasoning powder shows some promise.

Since the increase in the price of gold, the price of Ajinomoto has soared. In the southern provinces, because domestic seasoning powder is cheap and good, and its influence is strong, Ajinomoto has been greatly affected, and its business has plummeted. However, the Japanese are unusually cunning. Seeing that our Chinese people like to use domestic goods, if this continues, how can Ajinomoto stand? Therefore, they racked their brains to find ways to issue several other kinds of seasoning powder, such as Bai Ge Pai Wei Hua, Xiang Jun Pai seasoning powder, etc., all pretending to be Chinese goods, making a lot of advertisements, in order to pass off fish eyes as pearls and disrupt the market. However, unexpectedly, several of our domestic seasoning powder factories jointly published a newspaper to deny it. As a result, the paper tiger was exposed, and it was still difficult to stay in the southern provinces. Therefore, they had to change their direction and proceed from the Northeast, using their special influence in the northeastern provinces and the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Areas to invade everything. Fortunately, domestic products such as Guanyin Powder from China Chemical Industry Society and Weimu from Tianyi Factory had already achieved great success in sales in the northeastern provinces earlier. However, the competition between domestic seasoning powder and Japanese goods in the Northeast is becoming increasingly fierce! The Japanese believe that the Northeast is the base of Ajinomoto and other products. How can they allow others to snore beside their bed? Sure enough, Ajinomoto has planned to set up a factory in Fengtian to manufacture and advertise extensively, greatly reducing its price. Recently, they held a few days of parade advertising in Tianjin, which can be said to be a grand event. The purpose is nothing more than to wipe out our domestic seasoning powder in one fell swoop. Their scheming is truly extreme. However, in view of the current crisis, we feel that we cannot care so much about the matter. Therefore, I personally advocate that at this time of close combat, we must have a life-or-death battle. On the one hand, we ourselves try our best to improve the products and find ways to lower prices. On the other hand, we also hope that the Chinese people will assist, promote, and advocate! (Department of China Public School University)

Bamboo Branch Lyrics on Samsung Brand Products (Father) 153

In recent years, the national cosmetic products on the sea have risen like a storm, dazzling the eyes. However, most of them are of inferior quality and adulterated, falsely claiming profits. It is rare to find those who can manufacture excellent products and match the name with the reality. Based on my daily purchasing experience, the various products of the Samsung brand produced by the China Chemical Industry Society on Henan Road are the most popular among Chinese people. Now, on the occasion of the 20th anniversary of the society, I write a short poem based on my love for the society's products to introduce them.

Whose product is the best for brushing teeth? Samsung's national product is toothpaste. A handful of warm grease is fragrant on the cheeks, and the taste is even more abundant in the mind.

Samsung toothpaste. The fragrance is sweet and delicious, refreshing. Once you try it, you will love it. It is not only the fragrance of the teeth and cheeks. If you don't believe me, please try it.

Short Story: Sister (Wang Ji-huang) 154

Since I left my hometown and came to Hangzhou, unknowingly, seven or eight years have passed. What makes me the most reluctant and miss day and night is my parents and my sister.

Sister, her name is Ying; she looks very lovable. At that time, she was about to graduate from the elementary school near my home. Her singing and dancing, and her daily grades, were the best in the whole school. Therefore, she was praised by relatives and friends.

Recently, I went home, and I wrote a letter in advance to tell them when I could get home. Father had just gone out on business and had not returned. My mother, she was already leaning on the door and looking out. When I got out of the car, under the pressure of two kinds of emotions, unspeakable joy and soreness, I very hard called out, "Mom!" Mother smiled at me with tears in her eyes. I knew that Mother saw her son, who had been away from her lap for a long time, return home one day. Of course, there was a kind of stimulating disturbance in her mood. In a flash, my sister quickly jumped out of the door and still called me "Brother!" like a child in the past, and immediately dragged my hand towards the inside. Mother followed behind us, taking care of the coachman carrying my luggage. ···My sister is more and more beautiful, and her height is almost catching up with me." I sat and chatted with my mother, and my sister sat beside my mother. When she heard me praise her beauty, two red clouds flew on her cheeks.

Mother said: "Ying has been having toothaches recently. She has lost a lot of weight. Originally, her body was even stronger····".

Then my sister couldn't wait to say to me, "Yes! Toothaches sometimes make it impossible to sleep. And I still pay attention to hygiene and brush my teeth three times a day. Brother, look! How yellow and ugly my teeth are. What can I do?"

"Then why don't you use Samsung toothpaste? It's much better than ordinary toothpaste and tooth powder. It's cheap and it's a national product. Using it can make your teeth white and eliminate the danger of toothaches and cavities forever."

My sister used Samsung toothpaste according to my words for less than a few days, and the toothache stopped, and the tooth color also became white, and happily ran to thank me. I said, "Why do you thank me? You go thank China Chemical Industry Society! You take the heart of gratitude to me or to do more to introduce."

The Vocational Education Society Has Set Anti-Japanese National Salvation Measures 158

(1) Never use Japanese goods (2) Vigorously implement military training

(3) Vigorously implement nationalist education

Since the Japanese army invaded and plundered the Northeast, the staff of the China Vocational Education Society have organized an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, and the work is tense. The national salvation plan has been formulated and has been notified to all affiliated institutions to strictly abide by it. The original letter is recorded below:

Respectfully, this time the Japanese army occupied our Northeast in vain, burning, looting, and killing, which is inhumane. All those with blood and spirit are deeply saddened. The office of the society recently held a meeting to discuss and decide on the Anti-Japanese National Salvation measures. First, never use Japanese goods; second, vigorously implement military training; third, vigorously implement nationalist education. Half a month ago, the outlines of the anti-Japanese national salvation work discussed by all parties were roughly the same. However, in the implementation, the plan must be precise, the time must be lasting, and the effectiveness must be significant. Although the current plan is a stopgap measure to deal with the immediate situation, the fundamental solution is also here. The colleagues of our Vocational Education Society have been serving the society for many years, and in the face of the national crisis,

we should further promote the spirit of safeguarding the country and protecting the nation, and be the vanguard for the youth and the people. Regarding the item of not using Japanese goods, the specific plan agreed upon by the Shanghai Education Community National Salvation Federation is relatively complete and can be adopted. The badge and badge have been made, and you only need to collect, fill in, and pay for them. The procedures are very simple. Regardless of the institution, it is hoped that it will be implemented uniformly from today. However, it is essential to choose a day to convene an oath. The institutions in this city plan to choose a suitable time to hold it at the China Vocational School. All staff, teachers, students, and workers will gather at the same time. Those who are not in this city should also hold it separately. After the holding, it is hoped that the number of people who take the oath will be sent to the office of the society for statistics. Regarding military training, the regulations of the Xu Gongqiao Improvement Zone Youth Service Corps should be used as the basis. Except for girls' schools, it is hoped that the rural improvement zones and rural primary schools will implement it appropriately. The schools in the urban area should step up military training, not only imparting the equivalent military technology, but also cultivating the habit of abiding by laws and disciplines and valuing integrity. If it is done gradually and persistently, even if the problem of the three eastern provinces is resolved in the future, it should not be slackened in the slightest. As for the youth in all the supplementary schools, most of them already have jobs, and they can be appropriately added to the volunteer team for training. The responsible personnel should plan it on their behalf. Regarding vigorously implementing nationalist education, the first is to clarify the national shame and respect the national character, so that they can deeply understand the relationship between the country and the individual, and the thoughts of safeguarding the country and protecting the nation and the feelings of public-mindedness and righteousness will be revealed in their hearts from time to time. It is fair and reasonable to be friendly to those who are good to us and to be enemies to those who insult us. Now that the Japanese militarists have brutally treated us, we should be determined to avenge our shame and regard Japan as the only target. All schools, all improvement zones, and all places should pay attention to this point when implementing school education and social education. The specific measures are in the plan proposed by the Zhejiang Education Department, which can be fully adopted. The original plan was published in the Shanghai Newspaper Education News column on September 29 of this year. I hope you will check it. The national situation is in danger, and as for this extreme, all of us who are in charge of education should bear the corresponding responsibility. From now on, we should all deeply repent, change our past mistakes, wash away the sloppy style, and arouse the spirit of Pingdan, set an example for ourselves, guide the youth, save the country from danger together, and complete our personal duties. Ten years of training can avenge us. If one thing is done in a perfunctory manner, it is misleading the country. This is what I want to say with tears, and I hope to encourage each other with the loving colleagues of our society. Two copies of the specific implementation plan for Anti-Japanese National Salvation and the allocation of work, two papers of the specific plan for economic severance of relations with Japan, ○ papers of the blank voluntary book for not using Japanese goods, two copies of the regulations of the Xu Gongqiao Rural Improvement Zone Youth Service Corps, and two papers of the chronology of Japanese political aggression against China are attached. I hope you will check and collect them for future use. To: Jiang Hengyuan and Yang Weiyu, Office of the China Vocational Education Society, 20, 10, 18.

Free Talk

The Voice of Anti-Japanese Resistance

— Cai Liang

Recently, the Japanese newspaper Shanghai Daily News published a headline saying that our people's organized "Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association" is a "gang of robbers." I felt both hate and laughter when I saw it. The hate is that our country has reached the point of unbearable suffering, yet we still cannot fight them to the death. Even our people's "economic severance," implemented with shame and endurance, is subject to ridicule and abuse by others. The laughter is that the self-proclaimed violent Japanese are using the tone of a shrew scolding in the street towards our non-violent resistance of non-cooperation. Isn't that too useless? So, as I see it, as long as we carry out the work of boycotting Japanese goods seriously, I'm afraid it won't be long before we make the Japanese reach a dead end.

Don't Remove the Grass in the Courtyard: Sundry Talks by Zhai Fu

Edison's Death (Part 2) 171

Science should be a tool for nurturing and protecting people, not a weapon for harming and killing. Edison was hired by the US government during the European War to engage in special research. Edison himself said he did 45 inventions for the government; the government announced only 39, and it is unknown whether the remaining six are secret or if there was a mistake in the number. But based on these 39, most are for preventing and avoiding harm from the enemy. He created various defensive machines to subdue German submarines, much like how Mozi resisted Gongshu Ban's cloud ladder in the past.

According to the New York Times on June 24, 1923, the capital invested in Edison's inventions and the businesses they spawned in the United States alone was 15 billion US dollars (15,000,000,000 US dollars), equivalent to approximately 75 billion Chinese currency, almost equal to one-fifth of the pure gold mined in the Americas since Columbus's discovery.

The previous industrial revolution was due to the invention of the steam engine; the next industrial revolution will rely on the invention of the electric motor. At the beginning of this electrical century, there are several immortal electricians, among whom the most worthy of our respect are Faraday, the inventor of the electric motor, and Edison, the master of electricity who passed away a few days ago.

A Returnee from the Northeast Talks of the Ashes of Calamity 172

— Shi Yan Ye

Professor Peng Wenyu of Northeastern University escaped from the Japanese iron heels and returned south. Our school's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association specially invited him to give a lecture. After listening, I picked up some points to share with this publication.

After the Japanese soldiers occupied Shenyang, they brutally killed the innocent. A coolie was killed on the road. His wife, regarding him as her lifelong support, wailed over his body. A Japanese soldier passed by and saw it, kicking her to stop her from crying. The woman couldn't stop crying due to grief, and the soldier smiled sinisterly for a while, then his bestiality arose. He raised his gun and shot her. The woman immediately stopped crying, following her husband to the afterlife. The soldier then swaggered away. Someone saw four or five people lying on a bed, seemingly asleep, but upon closer inspection, they were all curled up in pools of blood. This proves that even if we don't resist, they will still devour us like ravenous beasts. At that time, the banknotes of Fengtian were like waste paper. Merchants refused to accept them, and the possessions of the poor were all this waste paper. Since the waste paper couldn't be exchanged for grain, they clamored in the market. The soldiers had an excuse to act. Under the guise of maintaining order, they slaughtered corpses filling the market. Alas, the people of Liaoning were the first to suffer the misery of being slaves of a conquered nation.

After the disaster struck, the faculty and students of Northeastern University scattered. However, there were still many who were caught off guard and unable to escape. A certain principal of a Chinese school established by the Japanese in Shenyang went to meet with Secretary of Northeastern University, Mr. So-and-so, being extremely attentive. He said that his country's rash dispatch of troops caused an accident for your school, interrupting your studies, which he deeply regretted. However, politics and military affairs are irrelevant to those of us who run education. Your school need not worry too much and can continue classes as usual. The secretary replied that the power of the oppressors was formidable, and the school's funds were all in the bank, blocked by the soldiers and unable to be withdrawn. The Japanese principal then said that he was friendly with the commander here, Honjo, and would intercede to help your school. He would return with

Mourning Mr. Edison's Passing 173

— Yi Yuan

October 18th of the 20th year (of the Republic). It was just a month since the Shenyang Incident, and war clouds were brewing in East Asia. The League of Nations was hoarse from mediating. Suddenly, another tragic news came, and the world mourned the collapse of a mountain. If people could be redeemed, who could call back his soul? Why did Heaven not pity and took away such a talent? Examining the glorious history of Mr. Edison, Ohio was his old hometown. The great inventor Edison's talent and fame spread far and wide. He devoted his life to science, disdaining worldly fame and fortune. Thus, he was able to strive and become a unique hero, his scientific achievements rivaling the work of nature. Sound and light have already been revealed in their mysteries, and electricity is especially infinitely useful. Modern transportation devices rely on his cultivation to flourish. Whether soaring in the sky or landing, his skills are amazing and unparalleled. He enjoyed a great age of eighty-four, his life full of extraordinary creations. From now on, North American electrical factories will continue to display his famous name. (Edison Electric Plant is globally known) Effort can always turn the tide, only devotion can accomplish great things. He always used this to instruct his disciples. May our countrymen not disregard this. Even now, the three islands are aggressive, and victory still requires scientific attack. Drive out the fog of Chiyou with cars, and turn back the wind of Red Cliff with fire. Alas, our Confucians are too indolent, and education is just beginning to enlighten them. Don't shed tears of Xinting in times of worry, raise a glass of wine to commemorate him by the river. (Response to Reimbursement)

Those who remained at Northeastern University, trapped under iron heels, were startled several times a night, with disaster striking at any time. They decided to escape immediately to avoid making meaningless sacrifices, all wearing coarse cloth clothes, looking like poor people. After boarding the Beining freight train, they all celebrated their rebirth. But halfway, they suddenly heard that the train in front had been chased and attacked by Japanese planes. The train they were on had also left Shenyang not long ago and was immediately ambushed by Japanese soldiers and bandits. Panic rose again, and they all thought they would become ghosts beyond the pass. The train sped through the terror, and only after crossing the Shanhaiguan Pass did it enter safe territory. Everyone raised their hands in joy, comforting and encouraging each other, saying, "As long as we keep our lives, we will sharpen our swords to kill the enemy."

General Zhang ceded the rivers and mountains, and the people of the country cannot forgive him. In fact, Zhang was upright and righteous when dealing with the Northeast in peacetime. In negotiations with Japan, he often said, "Diplomacy is a matter for the central government. I will take the central government's intentions as my own." Therefore, the cunning Japanese, wanting to act at their own convenience in order to steal benefits, were often blocked by Zhang and unable to succeed, thus harboring resentment in their bones. Once, Japan threatened to invite Zhang to drink, with warriors lying in ambush in the next room. During the drinking, Japan took out a secret treaty and forced Zhang to agree. When he refused, the warriors all came out, pointing their guns at him. Zhang shouted for his guards, who held their guns and confronted them. Zhang then said, "Leave," and the guards escorted him away. The Japanese stared in shock, watching him leave, unable to do anything. From this, we can see that this time's non-resistance was probably a last resort after weighing the situation.

A Good News from the Chorus of Resisting Enemy Goods 174

— He Pengfei

Because our country has suffered the bullying of the brutal Japanese, the people, driven by patriotic zeal, have launched a boycott of enemy goods. Theoretically speaking, this action can indeed strike a fatal blow to the Japanese. However, our country has boycotted enemy goods several times, so why hasn't it achieved good results? In reality, it only makes a few unscrupulous merchants richer. This is naturally due to the people's lack of sustained patriotic fervor and the merchants' greed blinding their judgment. But fundamentally, it is because many goods, even daily necessities, still do not have adequate replacements in our country. Even if there are, production is very low, and supply is insufficient. Coupled with the lack of organization in boycotting goods and the sabotage of unscrupulous merchants, the enemy goods are invisibly sold in the market again. Speaking of it, it is naturally a heartbreaking and tearful thing.

But here, I want to give a very simple example. Since the advent of domestic Wudi brand and other toothpowders, Japanese Diamond brand toothpowder has disappeared from our country. Doesn't this prove the rationality of the above? Therefore, I believe that passive resistance is temporary, ineffective, and incomplete. If we really want to resist thoroughly and forever, we must "strive for production." According to the text published on page 11 of this newspaper on October 19, the total amount of enemy goods imported in the year of the Republic of China in 1918 reached more than 340 million customs taels, of which cotton products accounted for the largest proportion.

Chronology of Japanese Aggression Against China and Various Massacres (2) 175

— Mo Yi

Year 22 of Guangxu (1896) (1) June 11th. Japan forced us to sign the Sino-Japanese Treaty of Commerce and Navigation in accordance with the Treaty of Shimonoseki, totaling 29 articles. In addition to obtaining various economic benefits such as inland river navigation rights, Japan also obtained consular jurisdiction in China, undermining the independence of our country's legal rights. (2) Beijing Draft Treaty. The content concerns the Japanese concession issue.

Year 24 of Guangxu (1898) Sino-Japanese Beijing Treaty. Japan demanded that Fujian Province and its coastal areas be within Japan's sphere of influence and not be ceded to other countries.

Year 26 of Guangxu (1900) After the Boxer Rebellion broke out in our country, Japan was the first to send troops to Dagu and later joined the Allied Forces of various countries, capturing Tianjin and Beijing.

Year 27 of Guangxu (1901) The Boxer Protocol was established. Our country agreed to pay a compensation of 450 million taels of customs silver. Among them, Japan received 34,793,100 taels, and the embassy area was delineated, obtaining the right to station troops.

Year 28 of Guangxu (1903) Japan and Britain signed an alliance treaty to protect all interests of both countries in China.

Year 29 of Guangxu (1903) Sino-Japanese Additional Treaty of Commerce and Navigation. Continued the Sino-Japanese Treaty of Commerce and Navigation of 1896.

Year 30 of Guangxu (1904) Russo-Japanese War. They used our land as a battlefield. After Russia was defeated, the benefits Japan gained were transferred from our country. All vested rights of Russia in China were ceded to Japan.

Year 31 of Guangxu (1905) The Russo-Japanese War ended. Japan immediately forced our country to sign the Sino-Japanese Manchurian Agreement, forcing us to recognize all the rights Russia ceded to Japan in the Treaty of Portsmouth, and opened 17 ports as commercial ports in Fengtian Province: Fenghuangcheng, Liaoyang, Xinmintun, Tieling, Tongjiangzi, Famenku; Jilin Province: Changchun, Jilin, Harbin, Ningguta, Hunchun, Sanxing; Heilongjiang Province: Qiqihar, Hailar, Aihun, Manzhouli, etc. And delineating Japanese concessions in the commercial ports of Yingkou, Andong, and Fengtianfu, and other various interests.

Year 32 of Guangxu (1906) (1) In May, Japan established the South Manchurian Railway Company, and began to implement economic aggression in Manchuria. (2) In July, Japan established the Kwantung Governorate and the Kwantung Army Headquarters, establishing the foundation for political and military aggression. (3) Sino-Japanese Treaty for Supporting and Collecting Taxes in Yingkou.

Total 117,811,000 Customs Taels 34.62%

The Pestle of Knocking on Dreams (24) 176

— Cheng Zhanlu

Chi looked intently and carefully. It was still the paradise of gentle breezes and bright sunshine, with no black wind blowing from beyond the sky. It was still the solid foundation of the Kaoshan Hall, with no signs of impending collapse. It was still the red-dressed, green-adorned singers and dancers, with no tears of jade or complaints of resentment. Pondering and pondering, thinking and thinking, the current happiness had not changed, so there was no need for him to call out for the abbot of the Wu'ai Hermitage. The moment this thought arose, it extinguished the exploratory electricity in the dark recesses of his brain, and he had already forgotten the Abbot of Wu'ai Hermitage somewhere beyond the clouds.

The dancers all came to inquire about the reason why he shouted "Wu'ai." Poor Tao Chi! How could he explain the reason, as his mind had once again darkened!

The dancers all danced together, also playing the music of Wu'ai:

What is Wu'ai? What is Wu'ai?

This place is great Wu'ai!

No past, no future, only the present;

This place is great Wu'ai!

Unknowingly, Tao Chi also followed their melody and rhythm, responding to this song of Wu'ai:

What is Wu'ai? What is Wu'ai?

There is great Wu'ai here!

Forgetting the past, throwing away the future, loving the present;

There is great Wu'ai here!

Tao Chi was infatuated with the present, truly "forgetting his homeland for pleasure" here! He firmly believed that this current Tao honey date could not be finished chewing even in ten thousand years. Who would have thought that a formless and silent blow would strike Tao Chi, making everything go black before his eyes? After a moment, he was able to open his eyes, as if awakening from a dream, still sitting in this revolving chair. The abbot in front of him, holding a wooden pestle for striking bells, had not yet put it down, only smiling coldly at him. And there was a faint lingering pain on his forehead. When he reached out to touch it, there was a lump the size of a chestnut, most likely a gift from the abbot's pestle! Alas! Where had the endless honey date gone? It had been replaced by a stubborn, irremovable bruise.
