Yarn and Cotton Last Week's Sluggish Yarn Market 181

Pessimistic National Affairs...Extremely Tight Finances

Sales are Increasingly Quiet...Consistent Decline

The yarn market in the past week has had a shaky and unstable appearance. Firstly, national affairs are in turmoil and unstable, and finances are extremely tight with silver discounts rising daily. Secondly, due to the silver supply this month, recipients are particularly lacking, and actual sales are increasingly quiet. Each group has no excitement, and the situation is getting weaker. Near-month prices are easing, and the decline in far-month prices is even more severe. Each month has broken the 60 tael mark. Fortunately, the market has a thin base of goods, and each factory has no intention of selling off. Although there is an extremely bad environment, it can still be supported for a while. Moreover, the anti-Japanese movement is fierce, the number of shipments is reduced, and the supply of local yarn is insufficient for demand. The future will also be a small extreme decline. Each group's purchase of spot transactions is very stagnant. The price of marked yarn for the near month is down 2.3 taels compared to the previous week, and the far month is down 1.2 taels.

Last Week's Marked Cotton Rose with US Cotton 182

The cotton market in the past week has been gradually rising. Because of the firm trend of US cotton and good transactions of Far Eastern cotton textiles, the situation is very stable, which has led to a帶 in people's hearts. At the same time, the exchange rate has also stabilized, so the buyer's minds are quiet. And a part of them think that foreign cotton may be temporarily stable, and they have greatly offset their short positions, so the surface is tight and the market trend is gradually increasing. And there are many mentalities that must look at four taels. However, spot cotton transactions are still light, and each factory has no large appetite. Because the amount of Indian and American cotton bags purchased before is very large, and the price is high, there is no urgent need to purchase for the time being, so the rise is still flat. However, Chinese cotton is higher than foreign cotton, so the rise is slightly suppressed. However, the current bullish attitude is abnormal, and the view and pull are particularly strong. However, the world's cotton production is still in surplus. What the future will be is still based on US cotton. In the middle of this week, each factory has bought a lot of foreign cotton again. The price of marked cotton for each month has risen by one tael and one or two qian compared to the previous week.

The Main Reasons for the Softening of US Cotton 183

Southern Hedging...Bullish Settlement

Yesterday, US cotton was initially weak due to Southern hedging, then firm due to inter-dealer buying, and finally soft again due to bullish settlement. Futures fell by two to seven pounds, and spot fell by five pounds. British cotton futures rose by nine points, and spot rose by eleven points. Egyptian cotton spot was unchanged. Indian cotton merchants sold slightly, and the market was firm and stable. Ping Guoer rose by 2.25 rupees, Aomu La rose by 2.75 rupees, and Bai Luo Creek rose by 3.5 rupees. Transactions were slightly better, but the market was also tired by one jiao. The foreign Dujian and Bianyin Yuan had no honor or disgrace. The Hekai cargo was 1,600 to 1,700 dan.

Silk and Tea Last Week's Silk Sales Still Had No Turning Point 185

British and French Silk Telegrams Did Not Improve...Sales Became Increasingly Weary and Stagnant

Silk Factories Unable to Support...Increasing Number of滅T Closures and Shutdowns

During the past week, the silk market of the local foreign firms still had no turning point. Due to the sluggish sales of silk fabrics in London and Lyon, Japan's silk was flooded, and Chinese silk had no appetite. The white factory business still had a market with no sales. Although New York had a telegram, the selection of goods was very meticulous. Irvines (i.e., uniformity) had to be above 83 points, and the recognition disk was increasingly harsh. The incoming price was surprisingly small. The A-body B-grade price was almost comparable to the B-grade middle-body. The factory had to lose 100 to 200 taels. The loss was too great and difficult to sell off. The European sales of Sichuan Qian 2 were also clear. Therefore, last week, white factory products only had supplementary transactions, with a total turnover of more than 200 packages. The output of current silk was less than 500 packages. The depression of the Chinese and foreign silk markets was increasing day by day. The silk stock of silk factories was increasing day by day. The turnover was無資. The silver supply was extremely tight and unable to support. The number of companies closing down and reducing their workers was increasing day by day. There were 106 silk factories in the entire Shanghai, and 48 silk factories in Wuxi. Currently, there are only about 60 factories working normally in Shanghai and Wuxi. There are less than 10 factories in Zhejiang's Hangzhou, Shaoxing, Huzhou and Jiaxing. During the week, the overseas Chinese silk price still tended to be flat and tired.

To the League Meeting 189

— A Female Student of Wanxi Futang

Since the East Province Incident, our school has been filled with an atmosphere of pain and anger. We wished we could immediately expel those violent and unreasonable "dwarf slaves" from the country. Whether in class or during breaks, no one could forget this national humiliation. Universities have all suspended classes, and their students are going out to promote, lecture, and petition, truly busy to the point of forgetting food and sleep. Although we have not suspended classes, we also have to do some work. Therefore, the third-year senior high school students of our school initiated a gathering of all students, asking them to write slogans, draw cartoons, and publicize the facts to male and female school employees in their spare time. However, in our work, we have adhered to two principles: "Saving the country without forgetting to study, studying without forgetting to save the country."

Since the slogans and cartoons were posted, some foreign teachers seemed to disapprove of this action. They sometimes said to each other that they were afraid it would become a successful mob. But our studies have never been neglected, so they had no choice but to accept it. Our school is a member of the International Student League, which holds regular meetings once a month. When the meeting day arrived, we naturally received a letter notifying us. But in this time of national crisis, who would still be in the mood for entertainment? So, the president went to tell the advisor.

"Mr. Ke, we are not going to the International Student League meeting today because there are other things to do at school," the president said to a foreign teacher.

"What, you are not going to the meeting? The spirit of the Chinese is too lacking! That's why your country has come to this state!" Mr. Ke said to her with a hint of anger and sarcasm.

Her face flushed red, and tears were almost about to fall, but she tried her best to calm down. Her gaze shot straight at the face of her so-called enemy, and she replied fiercely,

"May I ask, Mr. Ke, if your country were also in distress, would you still be in the mood to enjoy yourself?"

Mr. Ke became angry out of shame, and she said loudly, "No matter what, at least ten people must go!"

Tears streamed down from the president's eyes, and she was at a loss for what to do. So, she called an emergency meeting.

"Everyone, I never thought that our country has not yet perished, but foreigners are already treating us like slaves of a conquered nation! Today, Mr. Ke's order requires ten people to go to the meeting."

"We definitely won't go! Let's see what she can do! At worst, we'll argue it out with the principal, but we have a strong case. Who's afraid of her? Does the principal not distinguish between right and wrong?" Ping stood up and said angrily.

"Yes, I have the same idea as Ping," Zhao echoed Ping's words.

"Everyone, please listen to me. Yesterday, my older sister came to school to see me. She also mentioned the matter of attending the meeting today. I told her that we would definitely not go. She told me that the other students in our school were also not going, but the International Student League called and said that a foreigner who had just returned to Shanghai from an investigation in the East Province was going to speak today, and they hoped that all the Chinese would attend. So, they also joined. Since Mr. Ke insists that we go, and since today is not a social gathering, why not just send a few people? On the one hand, we can publicize our views to the people of other countries when we go, and on the other hand, we can settle this matter. Wouldn't that be a win-win situation?" Fen, who has always been afraid of causing trouble, offered this idea.

In the end, they all adopted Fen's method. However, those who went to the meeting all wore black clothes and were not allowed to wear makeup or lipstick. When Mr. Ke saw this attire, although she was unhappy, she only dared to be angry but did not dare to speak out.

Dear compatriots, we are already unable to tolerate being slightly despised by foreigners in our school. Alas, please think about the compatriots in the East Province. How are they being treated since the Japanese occupied them? Do they willingly accept it? If we want to wash away this shame, we must all unite and swear to resist foreign aggression. Compatriots, let's rise up! Strive, strive!

Book and Newspaper Introduction

An Introduction to Literature by Wang Yixin 190

By Cao Baichuan

Since the literary revolution, the Chinese literary scene seems to have been advancing at a rapid pace. In terms of creation, whether it is poetry, novels, or dramas, we cannot deny that there has been considerable achievement. Especially in novels, we can truly produce some excellent works. This is something that everyone cannot deny. However, books on literary theory are quite disappointing. Is it that everyone feels that literary theory is unnecessary, or do they feel that this work is difficult? Naturally, literary theory is an extremely necessary thing. This is something that those who study literature today are gradually realizing. But why are so few people doing this work? Naturally, everyone feels that this work is difficult to handle. Because to do this kind of work, if you don't have considerable research, you simply can't start. It's not like creation, where you can pick up a pen and write something, good or bad. So there are very few works on this subject. Even if there are any, they are just copying and piecing together bits and pieces without any system, just a mess of random compilation. How can they have any research and insights? How can they be called works?

Now, let's just talk about a book like "An Introduction to Literature." It is really impossible to find a perfect "Introduction to Literature" in China. I have personally read only four books. One is Ma Zonghuo's "An Introduction to Literature." Because the author of this book does not have a good understanding of the subject of "Introduction to Literature," the content inevitably has some inexplicable points. The second is Jiang Liangfu's "Lectures on Literature." Although this book has its strengths, the content is not pure enough. Finally, we must mention Homma Hisao's "An Introduction to Literature." There are two translations of this book in our country, one translated by Zhang Xichen and the other translated by Wang Fuquan. The content is still systematic, but it lacks insight. For example, when talking about the definition of literature, he makes a detailed copy of the doctrines of many people, but he himself does not come up with a clear definition of literature. So many people say that he is "copying and pasting," which is very accurate.

Now I want to introduce here a book on literary introduction that is very suitable for ordinary people to read. This is Cao Baichuan's "An Introduction to Literature," which was recently published.

This book is divided into the following ten chapters:

(1) Definition of Literature

(2) Characteristics of Literature

(3) Origin of Literature

(4) Elements of Literature

(5) Form of Literature

(6) Literature and Life

(7) Literature and the Times

(8) Literature and National Character

(9) Literature and Morality

(10) Literary Criticism

Looking at the above chapters, we can imagine the content of this book. Moreover, he also adopts Homma Hisao's chapter division method, marking many small subheadings under each chapter, making it easy to understand at a glance. Now I will briefly introduce the content of each chapter.

Chapter 1, Definition of Literature. He first talks about the literary concepts of scholars in China throughout the ages, and then talks about the reasons for Westerners' definition of literature and the reasons for the complexity of the definition of literature. Then, he talks about exploring the definition of literature from the elements and purposes of literature, and the various theories of dividing literature into two categories based on the two elements of thought and emotion. This chapter introduces the views of Chinese and foreign celebrities such as Pancost, Posnett, Hunt, Sainte-Beuve, De Quincey, and Zeng Guofan. Chapter 2, Characteristics of Literature. He explains the five characteristics of literature—truthfulness, infectiousness, beauty, permanence, and universality—very clearly, and also cites the views of famous people from ancient and modern times, both Chinese and foreign.

Chapter 3, Origin of Literature. This chapter first talks about the theories of the origin of art of the idealist school and the materialist school. Then, it introduces the theories of Shirakawa Hakuson, Mackenzie, and Morton. Then, it discusses the reason for the rhyme in primitive literature. Finally, it talks about the characteristics of primitive literature.

Chapter 4, Elements of Literature. This chapter discusses the essentials of the three elements of thought, emotion, and imagination in a very simple and clear way, such as the types of thought, emotion, and imagination, as well as their expression methods, etc. As for the "form" item, which is also one of the elements of literature, it is described in another chapter, namely Chapter 5.

Chapter 5, Form of Literature. This chapter first talks about the importance of form, and then discusses the key points of form. Whether it belongs to style or rhetoric, it is clearly discussed. Finally, it talks about the adaptation of form.

Chapter 6, Literature and Life. This chapter first talks about the relationship between literature and life, and then discusses the two methods of expressing life: realism and idealism.

Chapter 7, Literature and the Times. This chapter first discusses the close relationship between literature and the times, then talks about the new literature and art of the twentieth century, and then talks about the historical facts related to literature and the times, and the trends of literature and art. From classicism, romanticism, naturalism, to neo-romanticism, they are all explained very simply and clearly.

Chapter 8, Literature and National Character. The main points discussed in this chapter are as follows: the relationship between literature and national character 丨丨 the necessity of understanding national character in studying or appreciating literature 丨丨 the influence of race, which is the foundation of national character, on literature 丨丨 the preservation of national spirit by literature 丨丨 historical facts related to literature and national character, the differences in literature between Southern Europe and Northern Europe, the differences in literature between England, France, and Russia, the differences in literature between Southern China and Northern China, the differences between the literatures of fifteen countries 丨丨 the fusion of national character and its influence on the historical facts of literature, the literature of England and Tang Dynasty, etc.

Chapter 9, Literature and Morality. The main points discussed in this chapter are: important issues in literature and art, whether artistic or related to life 丨丨 the nature and relationship between art and morality 丨丨 the objectivity of art, the morality of artists 丨丨 the material of literature and art and the attitude of writers 丨丨 literature and art and propaganda, etc.

Chapter 10 is Literary Criticism. This chapter discusses the meaning of literary criticism, the difference between literary criticism and literature, the duties of literary critics, and the classification of literary criticism. Finally, it talks about six important modern criticisms: scientific criticism, ethical criticism, appreciation criticism, impression criticism, expression criticism, and social criticism.

The content of this introduction to literature has been briefly introduced. As for the detailed content of this book, please readers find a copy to read. I am responsible for introducing it here.
